# Spell List Index

An M or F appearing at the end of a spell's name in the spell lists denotes a spell with a material or focus component, respectively, that is not normally included in a spell component pouch.

**Order of Presentation** : The first spell lists presented are the lists of spells separated by class and level. These include the spell name and a brief and incomplete description of the spell. Immediately after those lists is a complete list of all spells with full descriptions of those spells listed. Spells in all lists are presented in alphabetical order, except when a spell's name begins with “communal,” “greater,” “lesser,” or “mass,” in which case it is alphabetized under the base spell name.

**Hit Dice** : The term “Hit Dice” is used synonymously with “character levels” for effects that affect a specific number of Hit Dice of creatures.

**Caster Level** : A spell's power often depends on caster level, which is defined as the caster's class level for the purposes of casting a particular spell. The word “level” in the short spell descriptions that follow always refers to caster level.

**Creatures and Characters** : The words “Creature” and “character” are used synonymously in the short descriptions.

**Communal Spells** : Communal spells function like other spells, except they allow you to divide the duration among multiple targets, treating each target as a subject of the spell. When you divide the duration, you must divide it as evenly as possible among the targets. Furthermore, unless the communal spell's description indicates otherwise, no target can receive a duration increment smaller than the smallest increment of duration listed in the spell description. For example, if you are 5th level, your communal spell's duration is 10 minutes per level, and you have four targets, each target must receive 10 minutes of duration. The extra 10 minute duration can go to one of the four targets or it is wasted.

- [**Adjuring Step**](ultimateCombat/spells/adjuringStep.md#_adjuring-step-): You can move slowly and safely and still cast spells, until you move quickly, make an attack, or cast a harmful spell. 
- [**Ant Haul**](advanced/spells/antHaul.md#_ant-haul-): Triples carrying capacity of a creature.
- [**Anticipate Peril**](ultimateMagic/spells/anticipatePeril.md#_anticipate-peril): Target gains a bonus on one initiative check.
- [**Blend**](advancedRaceGuide/coreRaces/elves.md#_blend): You change the coloration of yourself and your equipment to match that of your surroundings.
- [**Bomber's Eye**](advanced/spells/bomberSEye.md#_bomber's-eye): Increases thrown weapon range; +1 attack.
- [**Comprehend Languages**](spells/comprehendLanguages.md#_comprehend-languages): You understand all spoken and written languages.
- [**Crafter's Fortune**](advanced/spells/crafterSFortune.md#_crafter's-fortune): Subject gains +5 on next [Craft](skills/craft.md#_craft) check.
- [**Cure Light Wounds**](spells/cureLightWounds.md#_cure-light-wounds): Cures 1d8 damage + 1/level (max +5).
- [**Detect Secret Doors**](spells/detectSecretDoors.md#_detect-secret-doors): Reveals hidden doors within 60 ft.
- [**Detect Undead**](spells/detectUndead.md#_detect-undead): Reveals undead within 60 ft.
- [**Disguise Self**](spells/disguiseSelf.md#_disguise-self): Changes your appearance.
- [**Endure Elements**](spells/endureElements.md#_endure-elements): Exist comfortably in hot or cold regions.
- [**Enlarge Person**](spells/enlargePerson.md#_enlarge-person): Humanoid creature doubles in size.
- [**Expeditious Retreat**](spells/expeditiousRetreat.md#_expeditious-retreat): Your base speed increases by 30 ft.
- [**Identify**](spells/identify.md#_identify): Gives +10 bonus to identify magic items.
- [**Illusion of Calm**](ultimateCombat/spells/illusionOfCalm.md#_illusion-of-calm): You appear to be standing still, even when you take some actions. 
- [**Jump**](spells/jump.md#_jump): Subject gets bonus on Acrobatics checks.
- [**Keen Senses**](advanced/spells/keenSenses.md#_keen-senses): Gain +2 [Perception](skills/perception.md#_perception) and low-light vision.
- [**Linebreaker**](advancedRaceGuide/coreRaces/halfOrcs.md#_linebreaker): You gain a +20 foot bonus to your base speed when charging and a +2 bonus on combat maneuver checks made to bull rush or overrun.
- [**Longshot**](ultimateCombat/spells/longshot.md#_longshot): Grants a +10-foot bonus to the range increment for any ranged weapon fired.
- [**Negate Aroma**](advanced/spells/negateAroma.md#_negate-aroma): Subject cannot be tracked by scent.
- [**Polypurpose Panacea**](ultimateMagic/spells/polypurposePanacea.md#_polypurpose-panacea): Gain a relaxing or entertaining effect.
- [**Recharge Innate Magic**](advancedRaceGuide/coreRaces/gnomes.md#_recharge-innate-magic): You channel magic energy into your own aura, recharging your innate magic abilities.
- [**Reduce Person**](spells/reducePerson.md#_reduce-person): Humanoid creature halves in size.
- [**See Alignment**](ultimateCombat/spells/seeAlignment.md#_see-alignment): Pick an alignment; in your sight, creatures and items with that alignment emit a ghostly radiance.
- [**Shield**](spells/shield.md#_shield): Invisible disc gives +4 to [AC](combat.md#_armor-class), blocks _ [magic missile](spells/magicMissile.md#_magic-missile)s._
- [**Shock Shield**](ultimateCombat/spells/shockShield.md#_shock-shield): A shield of force protects you until you dismiss it in an explosion of electricity. 
- [**Stone Fist**](advanced/spells/stoneFist.md#_stone-fist): Your unarmed strikes are lethal.
- [**Targeted Bomb Admixture**](ultimateCombat/spells/targetedBombAdmixture.md#_targeted-bomb-admixture): Empowers bombs you throw to deal more damage to a single creature.
- [**Touch of the Sea**](advanced/spells/touchOfTheSea.md#_touch-of-the-sea): [Swim](skills/swim.md#_swim) speed becomes 30 ft.
- [**True Strike**](spells/trueStrike.md#_true-strike): +20 on your next attack roll.
- [**Urban Grace**](advancedRaceGuide/coreRaces/halfElves.md#_urban-grace): You become one with the city around you, allowing you to move more easily through its crowds and buildings.
- [**Vocal Alteration**](ultimateMagic/spells/vocalAlteration.md#_vocal-alteration): [Disguise](/skills/disguise.md#_disguise) target's voice.
- [**Youthful Appearance**](ultimateMagic/spells/youthfulAppearance.md#_youthful-appearance): Target appears younger.

- [**Restful Sleep**](advanced/spells/restfulSleep.md#_restful-sleep): Gain more hit points while sleeping.

- [**Silent Image**](spells/silentImage.md#_silent-image): Creates minor illusion of your design.
- [**Sleep**](spells/sleep.md#_sleep): Puts 4 HD of creatures into magical slumber.
- [**Solid Note**](advanced/spells/solidNote.md#_solid-note): Creates tangible music note.

- [**Invisibility Purge**](spells/invisibilityPurge.md#_invisibility-purge): Dispels invisibility within 5 ft./level.
- [**Keen Edge**](spells/keenEdge.md#_keen-edge): Doubles normal weapon's threat range.
- [**Litany of Eloquence**](ultimateCombat/spells/litanyOfEloquence.md#_litany-of-eloquence): Fascinates a single creature for 1 round.
- [**Litany of Entanglement**](ultimateCombat/spells/litanyOfEntanglement.md#_litany-of-entanglement): Entangles a creature for 1 round. 
- [**Litany of Righteousness**](ultimateCombat/spells/litanyOfRighteousness.md#_litany-of-righteousness): A single evil creature takes more damage from creatures with a good aura.
- [**Litany of Warding**](ultimateCombat/spells/litanyOfWarding.md#_litany-of-warding): You gain two additional attacks of opportunity for 1 round.
- [**Locate Object**](spells/locateObject.md#_locate-object): Senses direction toward object (specific or type).
- [**Locate Weakness**](ultimateCombat/spells/locateWeakness.md#_locate-weakness): You roll damage twice when you roll damage for a critical hit and take the best damage.
- [**Magic Vestment**](spells/magicVestment.md#_magic-vestment): Armor or shield gains +1 enhancement per four levels.
- [**Magic Weapon, Greater**](spells/magicWeapon.md#_magic-weapon-greater): Weapon gains +1 bonus/four levels (max +5).
- [**Nondetection**](spells/nondetection.md#_nondetection)M: Hides subject from divination, [scrying](spells/scrying.md#_scrying).
- [**Obscure Object**](spells/obscureObject.md#_obscure-object): Masks object against [scrying](spells/scrying.md#_scrying).
- [**Prayer**](spells/prayer.md#_prayer): Allies get +1 bonus on most rolls, enemies –1 penalty.
- [**Protection From Energy**](spells/protectionFromEnergy.md#_protection-from-energy): Absorbs 12 points/level of damage from one kind of energy.
- [**Remove Curse**](spells/removeCurse.md#_remove-curse): Frees object or person from curse.
- [**Remove Disease**](spells/removeDisease.md#_remove-disease): Cures all diseases affecting subject.
- [**Resist Energy, Communal**](ultimateCombat/spells/resistEnergy.md#_resist-energy,-communal): As _ [resist energy](spells/resistEnergy.md#_resist-energy)_, but you may divide the duration among creatures touched.

- [**Seek Thoughts**](advanced/spells/seekThoughts.md#_seek-thoughts): Detects thinking creatures' thoughts.

**[Ablative Barrier](ultimateCombat/spells/ablativeBarrier.md#_ablative-barrier)**** F**: Surrounds the target with layers of force.

- [**Acid Arrow**](spells/acidArrow.md#_acid-arrow): Ranged touch attack; 2d4 damage for 1 round + 1 round/3 levels.
- [**Alter Self**](spells/alterSelf.md#_alter-self): Assume form of a Small or Medium humanoid.
- [**Animal Aspect**](ultimateCombat/spells/animalAspect.md#_animal-aspect): You gain some of the beneficial qualities of an animal.
- [**Bear's Endurance**](spells/bearSEndurance.md#_bear-s-endurance): Subject gains +4 to [Con](gettingStarted.md#_constitution) for 1 min./level.
- [**Bestow Weapon Proficiency**](ultimateCombat/spells/bestowWeaponProficiency.md#_bestow-weapon-proficiency): Grants a creature proficiency in a single weapon for short period of time.
- [**Blood Blaze**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/orcs.md#_blood-blaze): 5-foot-radius aura that causes the blood of creatures in that area to ignite upon contact with air.
- [**Blood Transcription**](ultimateMagic/spells/bloodTranscription.md#_blood-transcription): Learn a spell from the target's blood.
- [**Blur**](spells/blur.md#_blur): Attacks miss subject 20% of the time.
- [**Brow Gasher**](ultimateCombat/spells/browGasher.md#_brow-gasher): Slashing weapon deals bleed damage to an opponent's head.
- [**Bull's Strength**](spells/bullSStrength.md#_bull-s-strength): Subject gains +4 to Str for 1 min./level.
- [**Burning Gaze**](advanced/spells/burningGaze.md#_burning-gaze): Inflict 1d6 fire damage to creature by looking at it.
- [**Cat's Grace**](spells/catSGrace.md#_cat-s-grace): Subject gains +4 to [Dex](gettingStarted.md#_dexterity) for 1 min./level.
- [**Darkness**](spells/darkness.md#_darkness): 20-ft. radius of supernatural shadow.
- [**Defensive Shock**](ultimateMagic/spells/defensiveShock.md#_defensive-shock): Electricity damages your attackers.
- [**Effortless Armor**](ultimateCombat/spells/effortlessArmor.md#_effortless-armor): Armor you wear no longer slows your speed.
- [**Elemental Touch**](advanced/spells/elementalTouch.md#_elemental-touch): Gain energy damage touch attack.
- [**Escaping Ward**](advancedRaceGuide/coreRaces/halflings.md#_escaping-ward): Grants extra maneuverability when you avoid attacks against larger foes.
- [**Fire Breath**](advanced/spells/fireBreath.md#_fire-breath): Exhale a cone of flame at will.
- [**Flaming Sphere**](spells/flamingSphere.md#_flaming-sphere): Ball of fire deals 3d6 fire damage.
- [**Fog Cloud**](spells/fogCloud.md): Fog obscures vision.
- [**Frigid Touch**](ultimateMagic/spells/frigidTouch.md#_frigid-touch): Target takes cold damage and is staggered.
- [**Glitterdust**](spells/glitterdust.md#_glitterdust): Blinds targets, outlines invisible things.

- [**Levitate**](spells/levitate.md#_levitate): Subject moves up and down at your direction.

- [**Stumble Gap**](advanced/spells/stumbleGap.md#_stumble-gap-)F: Small hole trips creatures.

- [**Summon Monster I**](spells/summonMonster.md#_summon-monster-i): Summons extraplanar creature to fight for you.
- [**Theft Ward**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/tengus.md#_theft-ward): You ward a single object in your possession against theft.
- [**Touch of Combustion**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/ifrits.md#_touch-of-combustion): Causes the target to ignite in a violent burst of flame.
- [**Touch of Gracelessness**](advanced/spells/touchOfGracelessness.md#_touch-of-gracelessness): Subject loses 1d6 + 1 Dex/two levels and is prone to falling down.
- [**Touch of the Sea**](advanced/spells/touchOfTheSea.md#_touch-of-the-sea): [Swim](skills/swim.md#_swim) speed becomes 30 ft.
- [**True Strike**](spells/trueStrike.md#_true-strike): +20 on your next attack roll.
- [**Undine's Curse**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/undines.md#_undine's-curse): Target loses its body's natural ability to breathe automatically.
- [**Unerring Weapon**](ultimateCombat/spells/unerringWeapon.md#_unerring-weapon): Grants a +2 bonus, +1 per four caster levels, on attack rolls to confirm a critical hit.
- [**Unprepared Combatant**](ultimateMagic/spells/unpreparedCombatant.md#_unprepared-combatant): Target takes –4 on initiative and Reflex saves.
- [**Unseen Servant**](spells/unseenServant.md#_unseen-servant): Invisible force obeys your commands.
- [**Urban Grace**](advancedRaceGuide/coreRaces/halfElves.md#_urban-grace): You become one with the city around you, allowing you to move more easily through its crowds and buildings.
- [**Vanish**](advanced/spells/vanish.md#_vanish): As _ [invisibility](spells/invisibility.md#_invisibility)_ for 1 round/level (5 max).
- [**Ventriloquism**](spells/ventriloquism.md#_ventriloquism): Throws voice for 1 min./level.
- [**Vocal Alteration**](ultimateMagic/spells/vocalAlteration.md#_vocal-alteration): [Disguise](/skills/disguise.md#_disguise) target's voice.
- [**Weaken Powder**](ultimateCombat/spells/weakenPowder.md#_weaken-powder): Targeted firearm's ammunition halves the firearm's range and imposes a –2 penalty on damage rolls.
- [**Web Bolt**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/drow.md#_web-bolt): You launch a ball of webbing at a target, causes target to be affected as if by a _web_ spell.
- [**Windy Escape**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/sylphs.md#_windy-escape): You respond to an attack by briefly becoming vaporous and insubstantial.
- [**Winter Feathers**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/tengus.md#_winter-feathers): Target's feathers thicken and fluff up to ward against winter's chill.
- [**Youthful Appearance**](ultimateMagic/spells/youthfulAppearance.md#_youthful-appearance): Target appears younger.

- [**Aboleth's Lung**](advancedRaceGuide/uncommonRaces/gillmen.md#_aboleth's-lung): Targets are able to breathe water, freely.

- [**Acid Arrow**](spells/acidArrow.md#_acid-arrow): Ranged touch attack; 2d4 damage for 1 round + 1 round/three levels.

- [**Enter Image**](advanced/spells/enterImage.md#_enter-image-): Transfers your consciousness to an object bearing your likeness.
- [**Eruptive Pustules**](ultimateMagic/spells/eruptivePustules.md#_eruptive-pustules): Acid boils burst when you are attacked.
- [**Excruciating Deformation**](ultimateMagic/spells/excruciatingDeformation.md#_excruciating-deformation): Target takes Dex and Con damage.
- [**Explosive Runes**](spells/explosiveRunes.md#_explosive-runes): Deals 6d6 damage when read.
- [**Fearsome Duplicate**](advancedRaceGuide/coreRaces/halflings.md#_fearsome-duplicate): You create a larger and far more menacing version of yourself.
- [**Fins to Feet**](advancedRaceGuide/uncommonRaces/merfolk.md#_fins-to-feet): Transform the target's fins, flippers, or tail into legs and feet, allowing it to walk on land.
- [**Fire Trail**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/goblins.md#_fire-trail): Flammable liquid oozes from your pores, dripping onto the ground and spontaneously combusting.
- [**Firestream**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/ifrits.md#_firestream): A rushing stream of fire sprays from your outstretched hand, dealing fire damage to every creature in the area.
- [**Fireball**](spells/fireball.md#_fireball): 1d6 damage per level, 20-ft. radius.
- [**Flame Arrow**](spells/flameArrow.md#_flame-arrow): Arrows deal +1d6 fire damage.
- [**Flash Fire**](ultimateCombat/spells/flashFire.md#_flash-fire): Ammunition in the targeted firearm creates a tremendous flash capable of blinding the weapon's bearer and those around him.
- [**Fly**](spells/fly.md): Subject flies at speed of 60 ft.
- [**Force Punch**](ultimateMagic/spells/forcePunch.md#_force-punch): Target takes force damage and is pushed away.
- [**Gaseous Form**](spells/gaseousForm.md#_gaseous-form): Subject becomes insubstantial and can fly slowly.
- [**Gentle Repose**](spells/gentleRepose.md#_gentle-repose): Preserves one corpse.
- [**Gloomblind Bolts**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/fetchlings.md#_gloomblind-bolts): Create one or more bolts of negative energy infused with shadow pulled from the Shadow Plane.
- [**Halt Undead**](spells/haltUndead.md#_halt-undead-copy): Immobilizes undead for 1 round/level.
- [**Haste**](spells/haste.md#_haste): One creature/level moves faster, +1 on attack rolls, [AC](combat.md#_armor-class), and [Reflex](combat.md#_reflex) saves.
- [**Healing Thief**](ultimateCombat/spells/healingThief.md#_healing-thief): You siphon half of all magical healing that the targeted creature receives.
- [**Heroism**](spells/heroism.md#_heroism): Gives +2 bonus on attack rolls, saves, skill checks.
- [**Hold Person**](spells/holdPerson.md#_hold-person): Paralyzes one humanoid for 1 round/level.
- [**Hostile Levitation**](ultimateCombat/spells/hostileLevitation.md#_hostile-levitation): Levitates the targeted creature up off the ground.
- [**Howling Agony**](ultimateMagic/spells/howlingAgony.md#_howling-agony): Screaming pain limits the target's actions.
- [**Hydraulic Torrent**](advanced/spells/hydraulicTorrent.md#_hydraulic-torrent-): Creates torrent of water that bull rushes any creature in its path.
- [**Illusory Script**](spells/illusoryScript.md#_illusory-script)M: Only select creatures can read text.
- [**Improve Trap**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/kobolds.md#_improve-trap): Improves one specific element of a trap chosen at the time of casting.

- [**Keen Edge**](spells/keenEdge.md#_keen-edge): Doubles normal weapon's threat range.

- [**Lightning Bolt**](spells/lightningBolt.md#_lightning-bolt): Electricity deals 1d6/level damage.
- [**Loathsome Veil**](ultimateMagic/spells/loathsomeVeil.md#_loathsome-veil): Nauseate and/or sicken weak creatures.
- [**Locate Weakness**](ultimateCombat/spells/locateWeakness.md#_locate-weakness): You roll damage twice when you roll damage for a critical hit and take the best damage.

- [**Magic Circle against Chaos/Evil/Good/Law**](spells/magicCircleAgainstChaos.md#_magic-circle-against-chaos): As _protection _spells, but 10-ft. radius and 10 min./level.

- [**Major Image**](spells/majorImage.md#_major-image): As _ [silent image](spells/silentImage.md#_silent-image)_, plus sound, smell and thermal effects.

- [**Comprehend Languages**](spells/comprehendLanguages.md#_comprehend-languages): You understand all spoken and written languages.
- [**Cure Light Wounds**](spells/cureLightWounds.md#_cure-light-wounds): Cures 1d8 damage + 1/level (max +5).
- [**Damp Powder**](ultimateCombat/spells/dampPowder.md#_damp-powder): Ruins ammunition loaded in the targeted firearm.
- [**Dancing Lantern**](advanced/spells/dancingLantern.md#_dancing-lantern-): Animates a lantern that follows you.
- [**Decompose Corpse**](ultimateMagic/spells/decomposeCorpse.md#_decompose-corpse): Turn a corpse into a clean skeleton.
- [**Delay Disease**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/ratfolk.md#_delay-disease): The target becomes temporarily immune to disease.
- [**Delusional Pride**](ultimateMagic/spells/delusionalPride.md#_delusional-pride): Target is penalized on attacks and checks but gains bonus against charms and compulsions.
- [**Detect Secret Doors**](spells/detectSecretDoors.md#_detect-secret-doors): Reveals hidden doors within 60 ft.
- [**Diagnose Disease**](ultimateMagic/spells/diagnoseDisease.md#_diagnose-disease): Detect and identify diseases.
- [**Ear-Piercing Scream**](ultimateMagic/spells/earPiercingScream.md#_ear-piercing-scream): Deal sonic damage and daze target.
- [**Enlarge Person**](spells/enlargePerson.md#_enlarge-person): Humanoid creature doubles in size.
- [**Forced Quiet**](ultimateMagic/spells/forcedQuiet.md#_forced-quiet): Target cannot make loud noises.
- [**Frostbite**](ultimateMagic/spells/frostbite.md#_frostbite): Target takes cold damage and is fatigued.
- [**Fumbletongue**](ultimateMagic/spells/fumbletongue.md#_fumbletongue): Target cannot speak intelligently.
- [**Hex Ward**](ultimateMagic/spells/hexWard.md#_hex-ward): Target gains +4 on saves against witch hexes.
- [**Hypnotism**](spells/hypnotism.md#_hypnotism): Fascinates 2d4 HD of creatures.
- [**Icicle Dagger**](ultimateMagic/spells/icicleDagger.md#_icicle-dagger): Masterwork ice dagger deals +1 cold damage.
- [**Identify**](spells/identify.md#_identify): Gives +10 bonus to identify magic items.
- [**Ill Omen**](advanced/spells/illOmen.md#_ill-omen): Target rolls twice for checks and attacks and uses worst roll.
- [**Inflict Light Wounds**](spells/inflictLightWounds.md#_inflict-light-wounds): Touch deals 1d8 damage +1/level (max +5).
- [**Interrogation**](ultimateMagic/spells/interrogation.md#_interrogation): Target answers questions or suffers pain.
- [**Jury-Rig**](ultimateCombat/spells/juryRig.md#_jury-rig): Removes the broken condition from the targeted object.
- [**Karmic Blessing**](advancedRaceGuide/uncommonRaces/samsarans.md#_karmic-blessing): The target treats one skill of your choice as a class skill.
- [**Ki Arrow**](ultimateMagic/spells/kiArrow.md#_ki-arrow): Arrow deals damage as your unarmed strike.
- [**Lock Gaze**](ultimateCombat/spells/lockGaze.md#_lock-gaze): Compels the target to look only at you for the duration of the spell.
- [**Mage Armor**](spells/mageArmor.md#_mage-armor): Gives subject +4 armor bonus.
- [**Marid's Mastery**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/undines.md#_marid's-mastery): Target gains a +1 bonus on attack and damage rolls if it and its opponent are touching water.
- [**Mask Dweomer**](advanced/spells/maskDweomer.md#_mask-dweomer): Hides presence of a spell from d_etect magic_.
- [**Mount**](spells/mount.md#_mount): Summons riding horse for 2 hours/level.
- [**Negative Reaction**](ultimateCombat/spells/negativeReaction.md#_negative-reaction): Targeted creature may not positively influence anyone.
- [**Nereid's Grace**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/undines.md#_nereid's-grace): You radiate the unearthly grace of a nereid.
- [**Obscuring Mist**](spells/obscuringMist.md#_obscuring-mist): Fog surrounds you.
- [**Peacebond**](ultimateCombat/spells/peacebond.md#_peacebond): Locks a weapon in place on the target's body.
- [**Ray of Enfeeblement**](spells/rayOfEnfeeblement.md#_ray-of-enfeeblement): Ray causes 1d6 [Str](gettingStarted.md#_strength) penalty + 1 per 2 levels.
- [**Ray of Sickening**](ultimateMagic/spells/rayOfSickening.md#_ray-of-sickening): Ray makes subject sickened.

- [**Reduce Person**](spells/reducePerson.md#_reduce-person): Humanoid creature halves in size.
- [**Reinforce Armaments**](ultimateCombat/spells/reinforceArmaments.md#_reinforce-armaments): Temporarily mitigates the fragile quality in targeted weapon or armor.
- [**Remove Sickness**](ultimateMagic/spells/removeSickness.md#_remove-sickness): Suppress disease, nausea, and the sickened condition.
- [**Restore Corpse**](ultimateMagic/spells/restoreCorpse.md#_restore-corpse): Skeletal corpse grows flesh.

- [**Shadow Weapon**](ultimateMagic/spells/shadowWeapon.md#_shadow-weapon): Create a quasi-real masterwork weapon.
- [**Sleep**](spells/sleep.md#_sleep): Puts 4 HD of creatures into magical slumber.
- [**Sow Thought**](advancedRaceGuide/uncommonRaces/changelings.md#_sow-thought): Plant an idea, concept, or suspicion in the mind of the subject.
- [**Strong Wings**](advancedRaceGuide/uncommonRaces/strix.md#_strong-wings): The target's wings grow more powerful, increases fly speed by +10 feet and its maneuverability to improve by one category.

- [**Cure Serious Wounds, Mass**](spells/cureSeriousWounds.md#_cure-serious-wounds-mass): Cures 3d8 damage + 1/level, affects 1 subject/level.
- [**Demand**](spells/demand.md#_demand): As _ [sending](spells/sending.md#_sending), _plus you can send _ [suggestion](spells/suggestion.md#_suggestion)._
- [**Destruction**](spells/destruction.md#_destruction)F: Kills subject and destroys remains.
- [**Discern Location**](spells/discernLocation.md#_discern-location): Reveals exact location of creature or object.
- [**Frightful Aspect**](ultimateCombat/spells/frightfulAspect.md#_frightful-aspect): You take on a terrifying, Large-sized form of yourself and emit an aura that causes creatures to become shaken or frightened.
- [**Horrid Wilting**](spells/horridWilting.md#_horrid-wilting): Deals 1d6/level damage within 30 ft.
- [**Inflict Serious Wounds, Mass**](spells/inflictSeriousWounds.md#_inflict-serious-wounds-mass): Deals 3d8 damage + 1/level, affects 1 subject/level.
- [**Irresistible Dance**](spells/irresistibleDance.md#_irresistible-dance): Forces subject to dance.
- [**Maze**](spells/maze.md#_maze): Traps subject in extradimensional maze.
- [**Mind Blank**](spells/mindBlank.md#_mind-blank): Subject is protected from mental/emotional magic and [scrying](spells/scrying.md#_scrying).
- [**Moment of Prescience**](spells/momentOfPrescience.md#_moment-of-prescience): You gain +1/level insight bonus on single attack roll, check, or save.
- [**Nine Lives**](advancedRaceGuide/featuredRaces/catfolk.md#_nine-lives): Gives the target the ability to get out of trouble and relieves harmful effects and conditions.
- [**Power Word Stun**](spells/powerWordStun.md#_power-word-stun): Stuns creature with 150 hp or less.
- [**Prediction of Failure**](ultimateMagic/spells/predictionOfFailure.md#_prediction-of-failure): Target is permanently shaken and sickened, and may gain a spellblight.
- [**Prying Eyes, Greater**](spells/pryingEyes.md#_prying-eyes-greater): As _ [prying eyes](spells/pryingEyes.md#_prying-eyes)_, but eyes have _ [true seeing](spells/trueSeeing.md#_true-seeing)_.
- [**Resurrection**](spells/resurrection.md#_resurrection)M: Fully restore dead subject.
- [**Stormbolts**](advanced/spells/stormbolts.md#_stormbolts): 1d8 damage/level (max 20d8) to targets.
- [**Summon Monster VIII**](spells/summonMonster.md#_summon-monster-viii): Summons elemental creature to fight for you.
- [**Symbol of Death**](spells/symbolOfDeath.md#_symbol-of-death)M: Triggered rune kills nearby creatures.
- [**Symbol of Insanity**](spells/symbolOfInsanity.md#_symbol-of-insanity)M: Triggered rune renders nearby creatures insane.
- [**Sympathy**](spells/sympathy.md#_sympathy)M: Object or location attracts certain creatures.
- [**Trap the Soul**](spells/trapTheSoul.md#_trap-the-soul)M: Imprisons subject within gem.

- [**Astral Projection**](spells/astralProjection.md#_astral-projection)M: Projects you and companions onto Astral Plane.
- [**Create Demiplane, Greater**](ultimateMagic/spells/createDemiplane.md#_create-demiplane,-greater): As _ [create demiplane](ultimateMagic/spells/createDemiplane.md#_create-demiplane)_, but larger and with more planar traits.
- [**Cure Critical Wounds, Mass**](spells/cureCriticalWounds.md#_cure-critical-wounds-mass): Cures 4d8 damage + 1/level for many creatures.
- [**Cursed Earth**](ultimateMagic/spells/cursedEarth.md#_cursed-earth): Plants die, living creatures catch diseases, or dead creatures rise as zombies.
- [**Dominate Monster**](spells/dominateMonster.md#_dominate-monster): As _ [dominate person](spells/dominatePerson.md#_dominate-person), _but any creature.
- [**Elemental Swarm**](spells/elementalSwarm.md#_elemental-swarm): Summons multiple elementals.
- [**Foresight**](spells/foresight.md#_foresight): “Sixth sense” warns of impending danger.
- [**Heroic Invocation**](ultimateCombat/spells/heroicInvocation.md#_heroic-invocation): Grants a number of creatures bonuses on attacks and damage, temporary hit points, and immunity to fear and charm effects.
- [**Hold Monster, Mass**](spells/holdMonster.md#_hold-monster-mass): As _ [hold monster](spells/holdMonster.md#_hold-monster), _but all within 30 ft.
- [**Inflict Critical Wounds, Mass**](spells/inflictCriticalWounds.md#_inflict-critical-wounds-mass): Deals 4d8 damage + 1/level, affects 1 subject/level.
- [**Mind Blank, Communal**](ultimateCombat/spells/mindBlank.md#_mind-blank,-communal): As _ [mind blank](spells/mindBlank.md#_mind-blank)_, but you may divide the duration among creatures touched. 
- [**Polar Midnight**](ultimateMagic/spells/polarMidnight.md#_polar-midnight): Cold darkness paralyzes and deals damage.
- [**Power Word Kill**](spells/powerWordKill.md#_power-word-kill): Kills one creature with 100 hp or less.
- [**Refuge**](spells/refuge.md#_refuge)M: Alters item to transport its possessor to your abode.
- [**Soul Bind**](spells/soulBind.md#_soul-bind)F: Traps newly dead soul to prevent _ [resurrection](spells/resurrection.md#_resurrection)_.
- [**Storm of Vengeance**](spells/stormOfVengeance.md#_storm-of-vengeance): Storm rains acid, lightning, and hail.
- [**Suffocation, Mass**](advanced/spells/suffocation.md#_suffocation,-mass): One creature/level suffocates to death.
- [**Summon Monster IX**](spells/summonMonster.md#_summon-monster-ix): Summons extraplanar creature to fight for you.
- [**Symbol of Strife**](ultimateMagic/spells/symbolOfStrife.md#_symbol-of-strife): Triggered rune makes creatures attack.
- [**Symbol of Vulnerability**](ultimateMagic/spells/symbolOfVulnerability.md#_symbol-of-vulnerability): Triggered rune gives penalties.
- [**Teleportation Circle**](spells/teleportationCircle.md#_teleportation-circle)M: Teleports creatures inside circle.
- [**Wail of the Banshee**](spells/wailOfTheBanshee.md#_wail-of-the-banshee): Deals 10 damage/level to 1 creature/level.
